<tr>
<td style="colspan:2;">
</td>
<td><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1063604349" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="navbar plainlinks hlist" style="text-align:center"><span>This box:  </span><ul><li class="nv-view"><a href="/wiki/Template:Muhammad_timeline_in_Medina" title="Template:Muhammad timeline in Medina"><span title="View this template">view</span></a></li><li class="nv-talk"><a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Muhammad_timeline_in_Medina" title="Template talk:Muhammad timeline in Medina"><span title="Discuss this template">talk</span></a></li><li class="nv-edit"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template:Muhammad_timeline_in_Medina&amp;action=edit"><span title="Edit this template">edit</span></a></li></ul></div>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Muhammad_in_Medina" title="Muhammad in Medina">Muhammad in Medina</a></div>
<p>A delegation, consisting of the representatives of the twelve important clans of Medina, invited Muhammad to serve as chief arbitrator for the entire community; due to his status as a neutral outsider.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cambridge39_122-0"><a href="#cite_note-Cambridge39-122">[117]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Esp_123-0"><a href="#cite_note-Esp-123">[118]</a></sup> There was fighting in Yathrib: primarily the dispute involved its Arab and Jewish inhabitants, and was estimated to have lasted for around a hundred years before 620.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cambridge39_122-1"><a href="#cite_note-Cambridge39-122">[117]</a></sup> The recurring slaughters and disagreements over the resulting claims, especially after the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Battle_of_Bu%27ath&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Battle of Bu'ath (page does not exist)">Battle of Bu'ath</a> in which all clans were involved, made it obvious to them that the tribal concept of blood-feud and <a href="/wiki/Eye_for_an_eye" title="Eye for an eye">an eye for an eye</a> were no longer workable unless there was one man with authority to adjudicate in disputed cases.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cambridge39_122-2"><a href="#cite_note-Cambridge39-122">[117]</a></sup> The delegation from Medina pledged themselves and their fellow-citizens to accept Muhammad into their community and physically protect him as one of themselves.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoI-Muhammad_18-11"><a href="#cite_note-EoI-Muhammad-18">[16]</a></sup>
</p><p>Muhammad instructed his followers to emigrate to Medina, until nearly all his followers left Mecca. Being alarmed at the departure, according to tradition, the Meccans plotted to assassinate Muhammad. With the help of <a href="/wiki/Ali" title="Ali">Ali</a>, Muhammad fooled the Meccans watching him, and secretly slipped away from the town with Abu Bakr.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124"><a href="#cite_note-124">[119]</a></sup> By 622, Muhammad emigrated to Medina, a large agricultural <a href="/wiki/Oasis" title="Oasis">oasis</a>. Those who migrated from Mecca along with Muhammad became known as <i><a href="/wiki/Muhajirun" title="Muhajirun">muhajirun</a></i> (emigrants).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoI-Muhammad_18-12"><a href="#cite_note-EoI-Muhammad-18">[16]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Establishment_of_a_new_polity">Establishment of a new polity</span></h4>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Medina" title="Constitution of Medina">Constitution of Medina</a></div>
<p>Among the first things Muhammad did to ease the longstanding grievances among the tribes of Medina was to draft a document known as the <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Medina" title="Constitution of Medina">Constitution of Medina</a>, "establishing a kind of alliance or federation" among the eight Medinan tribes and Muslim emigrants from Mecca; this specified rights and duties of all citizens, and the relationship of the different communities in Medina (including the Muslim community to other communities, specifically the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jew" title="Jew">Jews</a> and other "<a href="/wiki/People_of_the_Book" title="People of the Book">Peoples of the Book</a>").<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cambridge39_122-3"><a href="#cite_note-Cambridge39-122">[117]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Esp_123-1"><a href="#cite_note-Esp-123">[118]</a></sup> The community defined in the Constitution of Medina, <i><a href="/wiki/Ummah" title="Ummah">Ummah</a></i>, had a religious outlook, also shaped by practical considerations and substantially preserved the legal forms of the old Arab tribes.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoI-Muhammad_18-13"><a href="#cite_note-EoI-Muhammad-18">[16]</a></sup>
</p><p>The first group of converts to Islam in Medina were the clans without great leaders; these clans had been subjugated by hostile leaders from outside.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125"><a href="#cite_note-125">[120]</a></sup> This was followed by the general acceptance of Islam by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pagan" title="Pagan">pagan</a> population of Medina, with some exceptions. According to <a href="/wiki/Ibn_Ishaq" title="Ibn Ishaq">Ibn Ishaq</a>, this was influenced by the conversion of <a href="/wiki/Sa%27d_ibn_Mu%27adh" title="Sa'd ibn Mu'adh">Sa'd ibn Mu'adh</a> (a prominent Medinan leader) to Islam.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126"><a href="#cite_note-126">[121]</a></sup> Medinans who converted to Islam and helped the Muslim emigrants find shelter became known as the <i><a href="/wiki/Ansar_(Islam)" title="Ansar (Islam)">ansar</a></i> (supporters).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EoI-Muhammad_18-14"><a href="#cite_note-EoI-Muhammad-18">[16]</a></sup> Then Muhammad instituted <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brotherhood_among_the_Sahaba" title="Brotherhood among the Sahaba">brotherhood between the emigrants and the supporters</a> and he chose <a href="/wiki/Ali" title="Ali">Ali</a> as his own brother.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127"><a href="#cite_note-127">[122]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Beginning_of_armed_conflict">Beginning of armed conflict</span></h4>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Badr" title="Battle of Badr">Battle of Badr</a></div>
<link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1033289096" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_expeditions_of_Muhammad" title="List of expeditions of Muhammad">List of expeditions of Muhammad</a></div>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Patrol_of_Waddan" title="Patrol of Waddan">Abwa'</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/First_Expedition_to_Badr" title="First Expedition to Badr">Safwan</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Patrol_of_Buwat" title="Patrol of Buwat">Buwat</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Patrol_of_Zul_Al-Ushairah" title="Patrol of Zul Al-Ushairah">Dhu al-'Ushairah</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Badr" title="Battle of Badr">Badr</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Kudr_Invasion" title="Al Kudr Invasion">Kudr</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Sawiq" title="Invasion of Sawiq">Sawiq</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Banu_Qaynuqa" title="Invasion of Banu Qaynuqa">Banu Qaynuqa'</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Dhu_Amarr" title="Raid on Dhu Amarr">Dhu 'Amar</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Uhud" title="Battle of Uhud">Uhud</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hamra_al-Asad" title="Battle of Hamra al-Asad">Hamra' al-Asad</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Banu_Nadir" title="Invasion of Banu Nadir">Banu Nadir</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Expedition_of_Badr_al-Maw%27id" title="Expedition of Badr al-Maw'id">Badr al-Maw'id</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Expedition_of_Dhat_al-Riqa" title="Expedition of Dhat al-Riqa">Dhat ar-Riqa'</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Expedition_of_Dumat_al-Jandal" title="Expedition of Dumat al-Jandal">1st Daumat al-Jandal</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Trench" title="Battle of the Trench">Trench</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Banu_Qurayza" title="Invasion of Banu Qurayza">Banu Qurayza</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Expedition_of_al-Muraysi%27" title="Expedition of al-Muraysi'">al-Muraysi'</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Invasion_of_Banu_Lahyan" title="Invasion of Banu Lahyan">Banu Lahyan</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Hudaybiyyah" title="Treaty of Hudaybiyyah">Hudaybiyyah</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Conquest_of_Fadak" title="Conquest of Fadak">Fidak</a></li>
